Yeah like today one of my friends was going on and on about "bro that shit fucks with your GABA receptors so hard" and meanwhile I'm thinking "...actually it doesn't act on GABA at all..."


I enjoy it. Its the only thing that's helped with my anxiety since coming off a brutal 3 year benzo addiction. I thought I was gonna be too anxious to leave the house, or speak to people, forever. It helps me live a normal life and for that I'm extremely grateful. This is at 900mg/daily, never once have I been tempted to go above this dose. I didn't take any this past Friday and I was completely fine. Whereas, during the peak of my Xanax addiction, if I didn't have any all day I would be a MESS.


Some of the "withdrawal horror stories" initially dissuaded me from getting this prescribed, but I think there's a lot of over exaggeration going on. Most of the w/d reports I read are from people who have either a) never been through a REAL withdrawal in their life (im looking at you benzos and opis) OR b) people who are prescribed this but are also on a cocktail of downers, opiates, pain meds, benzos, alcohol, other meds etc and at that point, how would you even know what's causing what? I'm not saying this doesn't have a w/d component, but I cant for the life of me imagine it being as miserable as benzos.

> — I B Profane said:


I thought the method of action of gabapentin was unknown?


It could very well effect some subtype of gaba that is not typical of benzos.


> While the majority of GABAA receptors (those containing α1-, α2-, α3-, or α5-subunits) are benzodiazepine sensitive there exists a minority of GABAA receptors (α4- or α6-subunit containing) which are insensitive to classical 1,4-benzodiazepines,[8] but instead are sensitive to other classes of GABAergic drugs such as neurosteroids and ethanol.
> 		
> Click to expand...


So it very well could be an agonist of GABA, but your friend still wouldn't be quite right as it's exact pharmacodynamics are unknown.

> [dustball said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13048175)
> 
> 
> 
> 			How long does neurontin usually stick around in the urine?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — dustball said:

Borderline drug testing question, which isn't really allowed.... but I guess it's not *really* one since there is no good reason to ever be tested for gabapentin, it isn't scheduled, and the only place it's considered a drug of abuse is inside prison. Answer: Who the heck knows, since if you *were* being drug tested for it the duration would likely be similar to if you used the half life to calculate what a potential negligible quantity (or cutoff) would be. Since most drug tests (like for cannabis and heroin) don't test for the drugs themselves (except in impaired driving - and even 4-6 grams with no tolerance is less impairing than two or three glasses of wine IMO - or death investigations where the quantity in the blood is what is relevant), they test for the metabolites to confirm use, not *how much* you use. How long it stays will be based on how much you used, but my guess is that it is less than three days (with tiny tiny insignificant testable trace amounts present longer.  I base this assumption on the fact that wikipedia states that it is not appreciably metabolized and excreted renally unchanged, so there are no highly lipophilic metabolites to stick around forever like cannabis.


This is ALL conjecture and to be taken with a very large grain of salt. And why the hell would this be of concern? I'm only answering it because there is NO reason you would be drug tested for gabapentin and I'm answering it as if a purely physiological curiosity. Mods, forgive me if you see it otherwise and edit my answer out. People get tested for drugs not on the NIDA-5 when they get caught with them as a condition of parole or the like... gabapentin is unscheduled and easy to obtain, legally, in powdered form.

> Click to expand...
> — 40tuna said:


One of it's two indications is for treating neuropathy, and while a paradoxical pain increase can indeed occur with opioids (unlikely in this case as they mentioned it working with the hydrocodone).


Fibromyalgia is just a very poorly understood condition which the underlying cause not elucidated, and the neuropathy idiopathic (fancy word for doctors don't really know) it's possible their pain increased despite opioid and gabapentin treatment.


This is why I find paradoxical pain unlikely:


> "Summary Statistics
> 
> Reports of GABAPENTIN causing PARADOXICAL PAIN: 2
> 
> Reports of any side effect of GABAPENTIN : 32214
> 
> Percentage of GABAPENTIN patients where PARADOXICAL PAIN is a reported side effect: 0.0062%"
> 		
> Click to expand...


Now... if it increases when the hydrocodone is administered it could be a possibly, but it is more likely the actual pathology of the illness and not a side effect. Wikipedia lists "antipsychotics and certain anticonvulsants.[citation needed]" as causing RLS, and but it's wikipedia, has no medical citation, and if you don't have an irresistible urge to move them to calm the pain it's unlikely.


I wonder if the individual ever tried Nabilone for treatment? Just a quick glance mentions that as an effective treatment for some people suffering from fibromyalgia - it's a cannabinoid agonist (wikipedia says it mimics thc which I take to assume means it is a partial agonist, unlike some of the synthetic cannabinoids going around as recreational research chemicals).


IANAD, just my .02

**Gabapentin & pregabalin mechanism of action**


Its not a receptor that Pregabalin and Gabapentin bind to, its blocks the ionotropic glutamate receptor (NMDA) calcium channel which is what the NMDA receptor opens. Its pretty much exactly what Magnesium does naturally or what PCP does only pcp does it much stronger. When getting off these 2 drugs I recommend taking a good magnesium supplement lile magnesium citrate or magnesium sulfate or magnesium taurtrate, NOT Magnesium Oxide as it has like a 7% bioavailibility. Also probably avoid calcium for a lil bit. 


> [rangrz said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9860193)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I don't recall the specific receptor that gabapentin binds to, but I am fairly sure I recall that it is not the same as benzodiazapines. So taking the two together should not produce any competition for binding.
> 
> 
> 
> The two are somewhat related (mainly that benzo's and gabapentin seem to substitute partially for each other in withdrawal) though, and share a lot of the same effects... so its possible that using one may reduce the effect of the other due to tolerance, but that is just something I am deducing and may be incorrect on.

This is a very good drug if you know how to take it.  First off if you don't have at least 2400mg that would be 8 300mg caps. you are wasting your time.  If you do pop like 6 or 7 300mg cap with pop on an empty stomach.  It takes like 1 to 2 hours to peak and last for at least 6 hours.  It is a very social drug, very talkative, very happy, energized without the speedy feeling.  I got to know this drug from prison, in prison there was no opiates unless you were on your death bed, so Neurontin's were the thing.  They went for 50 cent for a 400 cap sometimes a 300 cap.  I would take like I said 7 or 8 and be straight all day in my cell.  One downfall though is you can't get high on it day after day you will build a tolerance very fast.  Best thing to do is dose every other day and you will be straight.  Snorting it has no better effect either.  Just take normal wait a few hours and you will be straight all day for sure.  Lyrica is it's big brother so if you get Lyrica it will give you the same high less pills to take, but like Neurontin you can't get high off them day after day you have to skip a day or two.  If you try to take huge amounts you are wasting it, you have to space it out.

Hello all. Short time lurker, first time poster. I find that Gabapentin works in my case, 300mg, staggered 1 capsule, each hour. I stagger that up to 900 Mg - 1200 Mg and it works great. Much stronger than 900 Mg's at once. I wait a solid hour or longer, then I take anywhere from 1mg to 3mg of Clonazepam. Then I feel real good. To whoever asked about Gabapentin and drug tests, I was prescribed Gabapentin in a drug rehabilitation hospital. I hope that answers that question. I also take Lyrica. 150mg, twice a day. I like switching between the two. Sometimes I mix them, but it's nothing special. Anyone know a good time to take the Gabapentin if you take opiates?

<!-- POST START: id=13367405 num=577 author=blue comet author_id=360372 date=2015-12-08T04:58:32+0000 -->
### Post #577

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13367405 |
| Author | blue comet |
| Author ID | 360372 |
| Date | Dec 8, 2015 at 4:58 AM |
| Page | 29 |

Fuck this medication.


Seriously. Fuck this goddamn pharmaceutical. 


I took it for 2 months at doses of 1200mg-2100mg per day when I was roughly 5-6 months off benzos and ambien and it has ruined my life. When I was on it, it caused major interdose w/d and horrible side effects (suicidal thoughts, major depression, severe shakiness, nerve pain, anxiety, weight gain). After finally forcing myself off of it without any doctor's help, and an urgency to stop due to the suicidal thoughts, I finally stopped the medication after two months use in March 2015.


Since that time, my life has been destroyed by endless withdrawal, both physical (shakiness, nerve pain, heart palpitations, akathasia, nonstop hair loss, stiffness) and psychological (irrational fears, derealization, anxiety, cognitive impairment, social deterioration). I have not been able to drive a car or drink alcohol & caffeine in over 8 months. This shows no sign of stopping, and the past few months have been especially difficult. 


The WORST thing about this is the fact that every doctor I go to does not believe me when I say gabapentin caused this. I have gone through hell all because I took a prescription by an outpatient center psychiatrist and it has ruined my life. I have never even gotten an explanation or an apology from them.


So, FUCK THIS MEDICATION. The biggest regret I have in my life is ever taking this shit. I just want this to fuckin stop already!!!!

<!-- POST END: id=13367405 -->

Hey blue comet, I am sorry to hear about your experience. I have read about similar cases of Gabapentin withdrawal. There is a thread dedicated for that but I guess you already know that one:

[http://www.bluelight.org/vb/threads/448441-Gabapentin-withdrawal-any-advice?highlight=Gabapentin](https://www.bluelight.org/vb/threads/448441-Gabapentin-withdrawal-any-advice?highlight=Gabapentin)


Irrc, there were some tips and ways to lessen these horrible symptoms, but that could have been in "Drugs-Forum" or the german board I frequent.

I will look for it and then provide you the links.


Can't you try to see a doctor with some printed papers of these withdrawal reports so he can help you?


Ironically other people report having no WDs what so ever after quitting Gabapentin. But I think that depends on length of use and dose. 

It is a strange medicine for sure and its mechanism is not even fully understood yet.


I hope you get better soon, hang in there!


Z

I have been on it for three years and it off and on provides more of a mood thing than a buzz. you have to continually take it when you want a buzz. take 1800mg, wait three hours and take it again same dose than three hours later take a slightly higher dosy like 3000mg.  For me i will go off it for a few days and this helps to bring back those feelings. i was hooked on it for a while, but because of its rapid tolerance usually two or three days will work and than lower your dose for a week and than try the bump up again. Works well for me. Maybe no one else. I also dose130mg methadone a day so maybe opiate potentate it a bit too.

Wow, I can't believe how many people don't get effects from gabapentin. I was an IV heroin and cocaine user for 7 years so I definitely know what feeling high is like and I get excellent effects from gabapentin in the 3,000-5,000mg range. It is actually more enjoyable for me than some benzos. Tolerance definitely develops rapidly but if you take a couple weeks off it will drop back off. Anyway, I came here looking for information on potentiating the effects of gabapentin. I skimmed the 24 pages of this thread and didn't see anything conclusive. Anyone have any ideas?

I've been jumping all over w/ Suboxone. 


I stayed on it steady for 6 months (for seizures) @ 1600/MG/day. I sometimes would feel "good" in the early stages but wore off quick (I was also on Suboxone and Keppra). 


just recently I decided to kick the GABA and have it for "good times"; meaning ill take 3200/MG one day rather than just take it steady every day. yes, this is the "druggie" coming out of me and trying to stop my own seizure meds (I have a brain tumor). 


anyway, I felt it was easy to kick although many had horrible stories. but again, I am scripted a lot of other drugs, so that surly helped. 


since being off GABA for the last 2 weeks I feel "normal". as if nothing has changed. just yesterday I took 4000/MG of GABA in the morning and had a good day. not sure if it was a GABA good day or maybe it was just a bit more sunny than it has been around here in MA; its been snowing/raining the other day was a beautiful, sunny day. so maybe the GABA changed the weather that day, lol.

<!-- POST START: id=13546341 num=610 author=jammin83 author_id=348022 date=2016-04-02T17:02:08+0100 -->
### Post #610

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13546341 |
| Author | jammin83 |
| Author ID | 348022 |
| Date | Apr 2, 2016 at 5:02 PM |
| Page | 31 |

Sup Sigmond ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


You are talking to a gaba junkie and I've been on it for about five years now unfortunately. Its a hella dependency for me and I get terrible withdrawals even when making small cuts/tapers. I've taken it many different ways, but after five years this med doesn't effect me the same as it once did. 


Are you taking it therapeutically or recreationally? I think you are overthinking it a bit tbh. I do stagger my doses sometimes if i am feeling extra anxious. I have a whole bunch of issues but this is the only med I take for them. I usually take the 900 mg all at once and im fine. Sometimes i stagger but sometimes I don't have the time. I know that's considered a waste to some but it works better than 600 mg at once for me. 600 mg at once will wake me up at night bc of wd. fun stuff. 


A small dose would be 100-300 mg.  Medium dose 600-900. high dose - 1g or more. with no tolerance 6-800 mg would be sufficient. I am prescribed 900 a day now but have been on 3600 a day. Didn't do much more for me on the higher dose, but I always took it all at once. It is water soluble. 


45 min might be ideal but 15-20 min works fine. You will only get a buzz for the first couple weeks but mainly the first few days. I don't think that's related to absorption just how it works. don't worry about the meals so much but it might work better. but even if i take it all at once im fine. 


After 5 years i get a buzz now but for a long time i didn't. not the same buzz tho. 8(


Theres also [this](https://www.bluelight.org/vb/threads/470294-Maximizing-Gabapentin-bioavailability?highlight=gabapentin+bioavailability) thread for reference.

<!-- POST END: id=13546341 -->

<!-- POST START: id=13546998 num=613 author=jammin83 author_id=348022 date=2016-04-03T00:22:30+0100 -->
### Post #613

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13546998 |
| Author | jammin83 |
| Author ID | 348022 |
| Date | Apr 3, 2016 at 12:22 AM |
| Page | 31 |

> [Sigmond said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13546436)
> 
> 
> 
> 			thank you for taking the time to post that; very informative and helpful. taking it therapeutically and just wanted to get the optimal effect per/mg.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Sigmond said:


no problem. 


I think its a good drug and I can't deny that it helps me a lot. I get no side effects but I think it has affected my cognition to some degree but I've been on it five years. 


You should know that it does have a pretty shitty withdrawal and some people have a really hard time coming off of it. Can be as bad as benzos. Some describe it as a combination of opiate and benzo withdrawal. It is pretty bad for some people and I've known a few that have suffered for over a year. Some people don't get withdrawals. But it all depends on how long you've been on it and the dose you were on and your own individual biochemistry. I would take breaks to avoid dependency if I could do it over again. I get totally destabilized if I cut my dose but I have other issues going on but i am pretty seriously dependent on it.  I do think it works well for me though so Im not trying to scare you but i think thats something people should know. bc withdrawal from these drugs can be serious shiz that can take a while to heal from if you are unlucky. sometimes it takes longer than a couple months. 


It can deplete magnesium levels as well. I would supplement with magnesium glycinate or something with a good bio availability. they both are calcium channel blockers and they can compete. you don't want to take them at the same time or it will mess with absorption.   


I do think it is a good drug but I just wanted you to be aware of that.

<!-- POST END: id=13546998 -->

Gabapentin has a fucking nasty dependency for sure. I ran out last month with this silly idea that I could just replace the gaba with kolonopin. I like that they fix my RLS so that I can function in teh day and sleep at night, but under no circumstances do I want to trade another addiction.

I was dopesick and had these as a safety net. I took 3.6 grams right away and an hour later I was set straight. Smoked some weed and went to the gym, when just two hours early I was hugging the toilet.


Held me all day and I woke up around 7am dopesick again. Staggered this dose and took 1.8 grams at a time an hour apart. About an hour or so later I started getting these weird brain zaps and jerking motions like my brain was skipping a beat. This has happened before if I take gaba for more than one dose subsequently, but I don't have a choice because it's all I have to hold me at the moment. I almost fell on my ass and nearly spilled water all over my laptop. My arms just jerk and I can feel my muscles doing it in my legs. When it happens your entire body just skips a beat.


Anyone else ever get that from neurontin?

<!-- POST START: id=13674236 num=624 author=theGirlWithBlueHair author_id=393824 date=2016-06-23T23:33:08+0100 -->
### Post #624

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13674236 |
| Author | theGirlWithBlueHair |
| Author ID | 393824 |
| Date | Jun 23, 2016 at 11:33 PM |
| Page | 32 |

That sounds like myoclonus.  At high dosages gabapentin inhibits GABA release and activates low voltage gated calcium channels and can become convulsant.  You're lucky you didn't have a full blown generalized seizure.  


The 1.8 grams you staggered was a MUCH higher dosage than taking the 3.6 grams all at once due to the bioavailability issue with gabapentin.  You should be more careful with your dosing if this has happened to you before as it isn't safe and can and will - eventually - lead to seizures and hospitalizations.

<!-- POST END: id=13674236 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=13674285 num=626 author=theGirlWithBlueHair author_id=393824 date=2016-06-24T00:15:28+0100 -->
### Post #626

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13674285 |
| Author | theGirlWithBlueHair |
| Author ID | 393824 |
| Date | Jun 24, 2016 at 12:15 AM |
| Page | 32 |

Yeah, if you took say 300mg every half hour, what it does is allow the full amount of the dose you take to get absorbed, so in theory, the full 3.6 grams would get absorbed.  Now if you took it all at once it's bioavailability would allow it to only absorb around only 33%.  The dosage you took isn't a lot.  Which makes me wonder why you're getting those effects at such a low dosage, as a lot people do dose upwards of 3600mg - and that's staggered too.  You must be particularly sensitive to it.  Especially since you only split it in half and took 1.8 grams all at once, an hour apart.

<!-- POST END: id=13674285 -->

theGirlWithBlueHair, has brought up an excellent point (very nice). 

According to [www.mayoclinic.org/diseases-conditions/myoclonos/home/ovc-20166171](http://www.mayoclinic.org/diseases-conditions/myoclonos/home/ovc-20166171) , myoclonos can be anything from hiccups to epilepsy(a metabolic condition) or a reaction to a medication.

<!-- POST END: id=13674332 -->

<!-- POST START: id=13674352 num=628 author=Nether Animal author_id=377382 date=2016-06-24T01:05:52+0100 -->

Now that I know what it's called, I've definitely had myoclonus before. I get it sometimes if I get forced awake and don't get enough sleep. If I'm really tired it happens sometimes. I guess I am just vulnerable to it.


EDIT: Tramadol made this happen once too, now that I remember. Maybe its a serotonin issue?

<!-- POST END: id=13674352 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=13674378 num=629 author=theGirlWithBlueHair author_id=393824 date=2016-06-24T01:26:38+0100 -->
### Post #629

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13674378 |
| Author | theGirlWithBlueHair |
| Author ID | 393824 |
| Date | Jun 24, 2016 at 1:26 AM |
| Page | 32 |

It's quite common surrounding sleep activity.


Tramadol is quite notorious for causing seizures.  It's activity at the 5-HT2C receptors is what mediates this, so it's likely it's definitely serotonergic with tramadol.  It also possesses noradrenergic activity on it's own though (in addition to indirectly disinhibiting norepinephrine release via the 5-HT2C receptors), and this could be an additional mechanism.


But with gabapentin, it's the "deinactivation" of the low voltage gated calcium channels and subsequent depolarizations that release glutamate and norepinephrine that are responsible for your myoclonus on this medication.

<!-- POST END: id=13674378 -->

### Post #632

|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13687724 |
| Author | theGirlWithBlueHair |
| Author ID | 393824 |
| Date | Jul 3, 2016 at 3:28 PM |
| Page | 32 |

Gabapentin will not really not like to cause an addiction per se.  It is not like cocaine or opioids. It is likely to cause physical dependence Physical dependence is just a state of physical adaptation your body develops towards a drug, it is not an addiction.


But psychological dependence can happen with any psychotropic medication, as well.

<!-- POST END: id=13687724 -->

Nope. You will get very little in the way of recreational effects if you don't take it properly. Taking large doses ends up with you absorbing very little, whilst taking smaller amounts over a period of time yields you getting much more in your system.

> — JackARoe said:


Good job being smart with low doses. My 90 day supply of 4x 800mg neurontins just came in the mail today (360 800mg gabapentins!!) so once again begins my battle to use my meds as effectively at the lowest doses possible while avoiding withdrawal.


For me, gabapentin at the dose I'm prescribed is *extremely recreational.* I know the way this medication interacts with my body extremely well. I can't put hot sauce on my eggs, eat them with mayo, and then drink a monster energy drink with my morning dose or I'll feel like I'm on a moderate dose of MDMA at work. I've been called into HR and sent home for being overmedicated when Ive done so.


Gabapentin brings death to any and all forms of social anxiety for me. I'm an insurance agent and it is absolutely no coincidence the way my sales numbers look. Without being too arrogant here, I'm regarded as being in the very top percentage of salesman in my office and am one of those guys that opts for all the pressure, strictly commission only, and make thousands of week for the vast majority of the time. Because the gabapentin takes all the anxiety and pressure from my job away, I quite literally at times chuckle as the managers increase the Heat on us and simply produce more.


My boss is well aware of what I'm prescribed and blatantly makes sure I'm not without my medication, as while in withdrawal from it... All my sales production goes down the drain. It's almost painful to make calls and attempt to close deals: I'll have three $1500 weeks in a row, run out of gaba, and take home $250 that week.


I'm probably the most dependent person on gabapentin on bluelight, as I rely on it to the point where I need it to make a living for myself and my fiance. Here in South Florida it is very well known that it is the best thing to have in your pocket if you're in opiate withdrawal and can't get your hands on any pills or heroin. There is a thriving black market for them on the street and I'm asked literally every day at work to sell my pills, which obviously I very rarely do as I depend on them so heavily.


So anyone thinking this drug isn't recreational needs to reread what I just said ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png) 


I would bet any amount of cash gabapentin will be at least Schedule V in the next two years.


*pops 2 800mg gabapentin*


im curled up on my memory foam king sized hamond and Rhodes bed on my girlfriends rather large breasts getting my ears played with like a cat with an erection as every hair stands up on my neck and back.


Happy gabapentin day to me!!!

I've been prescribed Neurontin 2400mg / daily for about 6 years running.  I'm coming off this medication and scrubbing a few other things off my list as well.

I was taking 25mg-100mg avg. Benedryl to sleep, sometimes combined with 4 or 8 mg of Tizanidine.  I tapered off the Benedryl and discontinued the Tizanidine as of two days ago. 


So far WD is what I would consider minor but still apparent.  I'm taking a B vitamin supplement and Mg 400mg early in the morning 2-3 hours before my morning dose.


Started at 2400mg and then tapered 300mg / day and yesterday I am down to 600 mg (divided dose).  This is what some would consider a rapid decrease but I'm experienced in quitting lots of things (nicotine, opiates, SSRI's, SSNRI's) so my take is that I taper quickly and listen to my body... if it's too hard to stand I slow down or move back up a rung until I can tolerate the WD symptoms.  Consider me not insensitive to WD's but experienced enough to be in tune with my body's reaction and know enough not to freak out at why I feel so strange. 


I expected the insomnia (it's not terrible, just difficult to stay asleep after a couple hours). 

I have had a few days where I've been very lethargic, and it's been hard to concentrate at work. 


But a strange and unexpected effect of the WD is that I have stomach pain.  A tight knot in my upper abdomen that may be gas, as it is somewhat (not fully) responsive to a dose of OTC GasEx (Simethicone).  Of course, two hours after taking Neurontin that pain also disappears.


So besides the Mg prior or well after dosing of the Neurontin, and besides Biotin (in my B- complex vitamin), can anyone offer any advice as to supplements or activities I could be doing to ease the WD's?


I'll be honest, after putting more than 5 kilograms of this into my system over the years, I am very leery of the phase that comes after the taper, when I have to come off entirely.

might be of no use to anyone in this thread but when it comes to opiate detox I can't speak highly enough of its superseded friend Pregabalin, aka Lyrica, - at doses of around 600-1000mg per day it crushes withdrawals & makes things much more bearable... - if you have no tolerance be careful cause it'll knock you hard for the first few days, eg: missing the doorway & walking into the wall by accident... but seriously, off label use it hammers R.L.S. & calms the nervous system tremendously plus induces great sleep to avoid the first 4-5 days of torture... - combine that with Valium, Clonidine, Naproxen & aggressive Loperamide & it'll make detox bearable... - then add magnesium, omega 3, Choline, Inositol, a high quality multivitamin, & large doses of Vitamin C, B1, B6, B12 & it's happy days compared to crapping yourself whilst shaking & shivering... - Warning, know your tolerances & be careful with the Valium & Clonidine as they will drop blood pressure & cause heavy sedation... - when detox is over & PAWS kicks in with lethargy hit the essential amino acids & get a script for Buproprion (Zyban) - a unique NDRI that targets expanded dopamine receptors to reduce fatigue/anehondia & can help quitting smoking too as a bonus... - personally wouldn't touch any other anti-depressants or anti-psychotics as they cause rapid weight gain & sexual dysfunction... (by no means am I disregarding SNRI's for other depressions ect, just not my cup of tea at all & i'm basing this on opiate addiction recovery)

I was given gabapentin for a nerve pain from shingles but I have been reading these threads and being cautious.  I took if for a week and stopped.  Low doses, 300-600 mgs. I was too cautious and suffered another week without any gabapentin.   But then I read an article that said shingles patients need to take an adequate dose, 2400-3000 a day. Actually loperamide never did squat for me either believe it or not.  My body says screw that to any BBB activity that may work. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  So all these cures or tools for withdrawal have been subjective to me. I was always under the impression anything that was going to effectively take away opiate withdrawal must somehow work on the receptors in the same way.  Maybe that is not true. It shouldn't be your liver as gabapentin isn't metabolized at all and is excreted completely unchanged in the urine.

**Nuerontin dosing**


Nuerontin is a great recreational drug.  I take it for anxiety and bi-polar.  Works wonders if I take it as directed.  SWIM discovered taking a large dose first would bring on a super chatty and energizing buzz.  The dose would be 3200 mg.  It takes like 2 hours to kick in but last all day if you take 800 or 1600 every 3 or 4 hours after your 3200mg dose.  The downfall after like two days of doing this the buzz goes away(tolerance).  On the flip side to that if you don't take any for like 3 days you can re- dose and get rocked again.   I have a hard time deciding if I want to do the as prescribed or dose every 3 or 4 days.  This is a on going battle every month.  I didn't know eating increased the absorption till today trying that now.  Peace.....

<!-- POST START: id=13734446 num=688 author=Keif' Richards author_id=161552 date=2016-08-06T13:50:22+0100 -->
### Post #688

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13734446 |
| Author | Keif' Richards |
| Author ID | 161552 |
| Date | Aug 6, 2016 at 1:50 PM |
| Page | 35 |

This is a little bit old, but I'll chime in. Gabapentin (Neurontin) has a wicked broad therapeutic index. I'm not proud to say this, but I've taken grams upon grams of Gabapentin in single outings on several occasions, either due to tolerance or the intensity of my Opioid withdrawal. Myself and others are limited in our intake by the fact that acute overdoses of Gabapentin - of Pregabalin for that matter - can and do cause some pretty intense, non-epileptic, convulsive activity, ranging from loss of motor control, to full body spasms and flailing sometimes resulting in injury.


For this reason, it's a good idea to not overconsume Gabapentinoids like Pregabalin or Gabapentin, but aside from these side effects, which seem to effect only a minority of the community, these drugs are relatively safe. They're even believed to be essentially safe when combined with CNS depressants (Opioids, Benzo, Alcohol etc.), contributing in only a minor, if any, way to respiratory depression. This argument, with my references, is part of what got me my Pregabalin prescription, despite having a documented history of pretty severe substance abuse; it's practically impossible to kill myself with this shit.


Long in a short, I'm sure OP is fine now, but, acute overdose with Gabapentinoids is definitely not in the same league as say Opioids or Cocaine, so your best bet, if you think you've consumed too much, is to let someone know what's happened, just in case something does go wrong and if you notice a marked increase in negative symptoms, perhaps consult a doctor.

<!-- POST END: id=13734446 -->

<!-- POST START: id=13736616 num=693 author=Nether Animal author_id=377382 date=2016-08-08T14:17:16+0100 -->
### Post #693

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13736616 |
| Author | Nether Animal |
| Author ID | 377382 |
| Date | Aug 8, 2016 at 2:17 PM |
| Page | 35 |

I've been taking neurontin sporadically for a year now, generally to satiate heroin withdrawal but also under the "hope" of recreational effects, although they don't happen every time. I've begun to stagger my dosage because I was popping up to 4-5g at a time and it just wasn't feasible anymore.


So I've notice that three things happen when I dose neurontin. Note that no matter what, it completely alleviates physical withdrawal. The only thing that remains is the fatigue, and neurontin can make that worse at times. Anyway, 1. I get the recreational effects. The drunk/staggering that is amplified by marijuana. Sometimes I get CEVs. This only seems to happen after a break in the dosing, naturally. 2. I get sort of high, but I get extremely jittery almost like I'm about to have a seizure. I've dropped and broken dishes before because of this. It's like my arms just jerk like myoclonus or something. I've never gotten a straight answer as to why this happens. 3. I get no recreational effects at all, only relief from WD symptoms. Upping the dose does nothing but cause fatigue at this juncture.


That's my experience, hope this helps. And does anyone else get the jittering?

<!-- POST END: id=13736616 -->

I never had any trouble with gaba withdrawal, in fact I've just taken 600mg from an old packet from a couple of years back, to help with diclazepam withdrawal. 

It was Lyrica that was a hellish nightmare to withdraw from. GP put me on a 12 week withdrawal programme and it was still hell. I can take one or two now though and they warm me up inside so nice, I'd have over any benzo. 


Giuppy, I'd recommend 1200mg for a sleepy feeling. I'm afraid they won't act like benzos or sleeping tablets...just make you feel heavy-eyed and groggy. Pop a cople of codiene too, to get you cosy.

> [giuppy said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13736893)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Thank for reply ,
> 
> also can anyone suggest me what is the safe gabapentin dosage for a good sleep and for how long I can take to  avoid addiction ?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — giuppy said:


Gabapentin is commonly prescribed 600 - 900 for sleep, but is prescribed up to 1200 in insomniacs or in those going through withdrawals.  I think gabapentin can be taken safely long term for sleep as long as you are only taken in once a day.  It's half life is only around 4-5 hours, so it won't be in your body long enough for it to adjust for dependence to take place.


But to be safe, I'd say 4-6 weeks.  Then taper off by 300mgs every couple of nights, just to be safe.  ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=13766140 -->

> [Nether Animal said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13736616)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I've been taking neurontin sporadically for a year now, generally to satiate heroin withdrawal but also under the "hope" of recreational effects, although they don't happen every time. I've begun to stagger my dosage because I was popping up to 4-5g at a time and it just wasn't feasible anymore.
> 
> 
> 
> So I've notice that three things happen when I dose neurontin. Note that no matter what, it completely alleviates physical withdrawal. The only thing that remains is the fatigue, and neurontin can make that worse at times. Anyway, 1. I get the recreational effects. The drunk/staggering that is amplified by marijuana. Sometimes I get CEVs. This only seems to happen after a break in the dosing, naturally. 2. I get sort of high, but I get extremely jittery almost like I'm about to have a seizure. I've dropped and broken dishes before because of this. It's like my arms just jerk like myoclonus or something. I've never gotten a straight answer as to why this happens. 3. I get no recreational effects at all, only relief from WD symptoms. Upping the dose does nothing but cause fatigue at this juncture.
> 
> 
> 
> That's my experience, hope this helps. And does anyone else get the jittering?
>

K


> [blue comet said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13763283)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I have gone through a horrific host of painful issues since taking gabapentin for seven weeks at 1200mg-2100mg per day. Lots of physical and psychological problems that haven't let up, and were not present in any capacity prior to taking gabapentin. Things like nerve pain, heart palpitations, exercise intolerance, derealization, irrational fears, inability to drive, nonstop hair loss, etc. It's been horrible, and this seven weeks of gabapentin use was in February - March 2015.
> 
> 
> 
> Anyway, I've gone to a bunch of doctors and specialists for it. Neurologists, cardiologist, internist, pain management, psychopharmacologist, etc. You name it. I've gone through a bunch of tests (MRI, CT scan, blood work, etc) and none of these tests have shown that *anything* is wrong with me. I have blurry vision in my right eye and have undergone several eye exams and it has shown no problem.
> 
> 
> 
> So, even if you still have lingering issues from your gabapentin use, it likely won't show up on any tests.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — blue comet said:


My symptoms sound less serious then yours thankfully. I am pretty sure that my kidneys are ok but I can't explain the joint pain in my ankles and wrists. I have a doctor appointment tommorow when I get the test results back I'll update this thread.

I had no idea of  the benefits of Gabapentin until I was prescribed it a couple of months ago for nerve pain. I'm already on Oxy, but that doesn't seem to help the pain from nerve damage in my right leg (I've had 3 hip surgeries, 2 of which were replacements). Anyway, Gaba doesn't mess me up the way a high dose of Oxy does, but it definitely helps! I do find it works best if I take a week or so off every month so my tolerance can drop, but I've never noticed any w/d, and I usually take up to 1800mg/day. I do like the mellowing side effects, I must say. I know everyone responds differently, this is just my experience. I can say that the nerve pain is much more noticeable without it!

<!-- POST END: id=13780216 -->

When I was hooked on gabapentin,  and I got WD symptoms,  I noticed the most noticeable ones were: sweating,  SPACINESS, confusion,  nausea,  and anxiety/panic attacks, and nightmares when sleeping. It didn't last very long though, and went away within several days,  but the anxiety/panic attacks stuck around for quite a while until I got my script refilled. 


I am now very careful with them,  I only take them as needed,  and sometimes don't take any for several days at a time.  And those days I don't take any I don't notice any WD symptoms.

<!-- POST END: id=13780926 -->

**Gabapentin Headaches**


So I've been getting a decent amount of relief from my Post Treatment Lyme Disease Syndrome symptoms from gabapentin, taken at night to help with insomnia and resulting fatigue.  But the past three nights I had a headache every time, about thirty minutes after I took my gabapentin.  I also noticed that the headache came on each time after I started masturbating (sorry for the TMI, but I think it might be relevant) and I looked up sex headaches, which is apparently a thing.  This morning I also have a similar headache.  I'm hoping that the headache is not related to the gabapentin but I wanted to check to see if that is a common occurence.  

It was on the back of my head on the right side where I felt most of the pain.  It went away after one ibuprofen if that gives a good estimate of how severe.

Is this something that's possibly a dangerous side-effect of gabapentin?  Or is it more likely a coincidence?  My dad has migraine syndrome (I think?) which manifests not only with migraines but with all sorts of minor headaches etc...  Maybe I'm just genetically prone to headaches with varied triggers?

What should I do?

I'm prescribed gabapentin 600mgs 4x daily. At most, it takes away about 20% of my nerve pain. So, obviously I am a little underwhelmed with it.....but, it's the best nerve pain killer that I've been prescribed...so I continue to take it.


But recently my AWESOME pain doctor(who truly cares about my health) started a whole new "section" in his pain practice.....Ketamine infusions....OH MY GOD it fucking works 1000% and lasts a couple weeks(at least for me, it varies from person to person....for some people it lasts a whole year). I simply go to my doctors office and sit in a nice comfy armchair and they put an IV in me and give me an infusion of ketamine for about an hour. It makes you trip balls and feel AMAZING euphoria(like you would expect from pure medical grade IV ketamine) and then I have someone drive me home.....very easy. 


....I highly recommend Ketamine infusions. Maybe you can find someone near you who does it. 


Good luck,


jB


*WARNING....the ketamine acts like a truth serum, except you just spout shit out without anyone having to ask you questions.....so be careful if you are more on the private side*

> — JoeJunky said:


First of all the infusions are not an attempt to get you high. They are meant to be treatments for nerve pain(among other things) and so the goal isn't to get fucked up. I also highly doubt the doses of ketamine you got in the hospital were the same as I received during my infusion. The ketamine is being used for 2 totally different reasons in those scenarios.


Secondly...I found that the ketamine infusions actually were VERY potent and noticeably stronger than the street ketamine use I've used(which was quite pure and strong enough to cause the "k-hole" effect). For example, for the majority of my infusion, I felt as if I were traveling between and throughout different dimensions and worlds....into the past and forward into the future. In, my opinion, if it were any stronger, I don't think I would have enjoyed it. 

My doc said that 9 out of 10 patients having infusions pass out the whole time(which I witnessed during my infusion...the lady being infused next to me)...but I was fully awake the whole time...I just may not have felt like I was currently on planet earth. 


*My doc didn't "jump' me from gabapentin to Ketamine. I'm still prescribed the gabapentin, it's just the health benefits from the ketamine infusions are too good to pass on. I also had complete control over whether I wanted to try the infusions or not.*

<!-- POST START: id=13924708 num=764 author=Breathe author_id=119389 date=2017-01-24T23:43:44+0000 -->
### Post #764

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13924708 |
| Author | Breathe |
| Author ID | 119389 |
| Date | Jan 24, 2017 at 11:43 PM |
| Page | 39 |

Okay, so


I've been taking Gabapentin for the past 5 years, on and off..

but only during times that involve heroin withdrawal 

and the subsequent PAWS symptoms.


It is a magical substance, in my opinion, 

in that it totally kills RLS symptoms, 

the hot/cold flashes, 

and nervous anxiety that accompany opiate withdrawal..


It has no side effects that I would consider "bad".  

Even the withdrawal from it is very easy, when weaned properly.  

(I do not recommend daily Gabapentin unless you need it.)


Now, because of said experiences, 

I have also had it available for recreational use - and let me tell you, 

I really like it.  I really like how a small amount can be used

to *augment *a situation, for me.  

Instead of getting irrevocably fucked up,

I can get a smooth, even buzz from it and not have a crash, or any such thing.


This is NOT a drug that utterly consumes you 

or really *forces* the high - like Heroin or even Alcohol.

But I believe it can be psychologically addictive, especially if used daily

(daily use would include physical addiction, too)


In low/moderate doses (300-1200), Gabapentin is an excellent booster for my social interaction, and even studying.

At 1200mg, I get a warm glow and feel relaxed.  If I'm in a social situation, I even get hyper, jokey, and enthusiastic.

If I'm at home and not interacting, I just feel really chill.  Like the feeling after a good meditation session.


At high doses around 1800 and up, I get the above mentioned effects but much heavier and 

followed by some unccomfortable sedation. 


I once took around 3600 once, when I was kicking H. and had no money..

It suffices to say that I felt similar

to times I had chugged a lot of vodka...

 I felt shit-faced, and while it took away

my withdrawals, I did not like that feeling.


Lyrica - I took two 50mg caps once, while at work.  HUGE mistake.  I was so fucked up I couldn't even write my evening report

before leaving work.  I had to call a friend who lived nearby to come write it out for me. lol. 

It was like high-powered, no-nonsense Gabapentin.


Potentiation - Gabapentin takes a while to kick in, for me.  

About 2 hours to fully feel it.  

So I experimented and found 

that taking it on an empty stomach helps, with water 

- followed by a cup of coffee 10min later 

- followed by a cup of coconut milk 30min later. 

(Not sure why that helps, but that is my routine.)


Kratom - on certain days, I like to do the above routine, 

and then when I drink the coconut milk,

I add in about 3g of Maeng Da Kratom.  

That usually results in a very relaxed, happy, warm feeling.


Ginko Biloba - I take this at the coconut stage, if I need to study 

or am going to work.  Super clear thinking. Add Kratom and I get that plus energy.


It really just depends on what I'm doing when I decide to do this.

That factor determines which supplements I will take with it.

If you have any questions about this, PM me.


Take care, be careful.

<!-- POST END: id=13924708 -->

After reading through this thread... I did a few tries:

First time: took six 100s, took three more every 30 minutes, until I took a total of 1500mg

Results: mild "drunk" feeling, quite a bit of dizziness and clumsiness (could NOT) find my footing, then weird extremely cool visual hallucinations when I closed my eyes-- like I was above ground flying through trees, looking down at the landscapes, it was all passing so quickly that I could feel my eyes looking down to try to focus on what was soon passing.


Second time: started with nine 100s, took three more ever 20 minutes, until I took a total of 2000 (Ran out)

Results: Completely out of my mind- spent about an hour applying layers of makeup and trying to "contour" my face (I typically don't fuss with makeup), went to town cleaning my apartment (something I NEVER do), spent A LOT of time bonding with my cats (quite enjoyable), and time-took-so-long. Not in a bad way. It was like I had all the time in the world to do whatever I wanted. Did have balance issues, pupils were quite dialated, and eyes were blood red (could be bc I didn't sleep a wink). 


Now I'm just upset I told my pain management specialist that it did nothing for my pain ... Seeing some value in it now...


Good luck!

I can tell a difference in my pain when I miss taking the gabapentin that's for sure. Hope this helps someone somehow.

**Dosing Question For Gabapentin After Short Tolerance Break!**


So I've been taking Gabapentin the last two weeks. First few days, I took 300mg a day, few days later 600mg a day for about a week, and now I've taken 800mg a day for the last 3 days.


Overall haven't been on Gabapentin long, but my question is, if I take a 5-6 day break from it, would I be able to handle one 800mg Gabapentin for my first time again for close to a week?


I started creating a tolerance and now want to give it close to a week before trying again, but am nervous to start with 800mg. That's all I have too.


I can start by breaking it in half to make 400mg and seeing where that gets me, but if it doesn't seem like enough and i take another 400mg, I'm afraid that'll also be too much due to bioavailability being stronger with low doses every 30-60 minutes.

So I'm a little conflicted here. Any suggestions or advice on this matter? Or do you think 800mg would be just enough considering that's what I was just doing for little time.


Im at 22 year old male weighing around 155lbs if that helps any.

Everybody is different. I've been put on gabapentin a few different times. 300mg, 3x p/day. The last couple of times I experienced extreme euphoria quite unlike anything I've experienced before that lasted well into the next day. This went on for about a week each time perscribed. Now I was extremely clumsy and forgetful as well. I build up a tolerance to drugs very quickly and that is definitely true with gabapentin and many users. To this day I wonder why it hit me like it did. I have an autonomic disorder and my body often reacts abnormally 2 most things. Maybe that's it?

<!-- POST START: id=13945583 num=771 author=crazy hillbilly author_id=438040 date=2017-02-10T16:40:52+0000 -->
### Post #771

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13945583 |
| Author | crazy hillbilly |
| Author ID | 438040 |
| Date | Feb 10, 2017 at 4:40 PM |
| Page | 39 |

People are pretty naive on the topic of Gabapentin. Some think it's similar to benzos, others think it's a potentiator for opiates, both are false. As it applies to opiates, Gabapentin increases bio-availability for certain opiates, it does not potentiate their effects. As far as being comparble to benzos, in high enough doses it can produce an effect similar to a benzo trance, but isnt related to benzos in any conceivable way. What gabapentin will do is potentiate other drugs like Meth or MDMA, drugs that affect GABA lvl's in the brain, hence GABA-pentin.

<!-- POST END: id=13945583 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=13945589 num=772 author=crazy hillbilly author_id=438040 date=2017-02-10T16:46:11+0000 -->

I should add that when used as a potentiator for substance like meth, the combined effects can be

deadly. I do not condone or advocate the use of that drug for any other reason than for what it's intended use is. To do otherwise is dangerous and reckless, and if you consider it, get to a mental health professional ASAP, as there is something seriously wrong with your nugget.

<!-- POST START: id=13981958 num=777 author=Ravex24 author_id=442291 date=2017-03-16T13:37:12+0000 -->
### Post #777

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13981958 |
| Author | Ravex24 |
| Author ID | 442291 |
| Date | Mar 16, 2017 at 1:37 PM |
| Page | 39 |

I have done a lot of research and a lot of experimentation with Gabapentin. So, here's what I found: I used to take 4.2g-4.8g, starting with 3 600mg pills and spacing the dose out every 30 min. after. This got me that desired euphoric, energetic but calm, clear-headed, numbing effect that I desired. I always took with soda. However, what I found is that I can get the same effect on much lower doses. After trial and error, I found that if I take Aleve (or something similar) 30 min before my first dose, I can start with 300mg then space out that same dosing for about 45 min each time, while drinking soda. I do this until I have reached 1200mg and then I eat well and I can get very similar effects to that of my 4.2-4.8g days. I can also take some more but it seems like the intensity of each one isn't as strong as the previous ones, though it does increase the effects a little bit. Remember, this thing takes a while to kick in, so give it some time. Usually I peak at 2-4 hours and then stay that way for about 12 hours. Tolerance will build up quick so I try to wait 24 hrs after the effects have worn off before doing this again so that I get similar effects every time. I have never had any negative side effects or withdrawals from this and I have been doing this routine for about a half a year with only 2 week breaks every 2 months. Remember, everybody is different, though. I will continue to experiment and post again if I find something new that helps lower dosage or increases the effects. Have fun and be safe in whatever you do.

<!-- POST END: id=13981958 -->

<!-- POST START: id=13996762 num=780 author=Tralfaz author_id=444156 date=2017-03-31T20:09:41+0100 -->
### Post #780

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13996762 |
| Author | Tralfaz |
| Author ID | 444156 |
| Date | Mar 31, 2017 at 8:09 PM |
| Page | 39 |

I take gabapentin for nerve pain and oxycodone for break trough relief for degenerative lumbar discs. If you're looking for the ultimate buzz using your gabapentin prescription, this is what I have come up with after some serious trial and error with gabapentin dosages and percocets. 

Large and small.

Staggering a gabapentin 300mg dosage once or twice per hour works best for me. Start the gabapentin off early in the am. Like 4am  Do that for about six or seven hours or so , then drop a few 10mg percocets on that mellow gabapentin buzz you should be feeling after using the staggering method. In another hour,you'll feel just fine the rest of the day. Just a mellow yellow buzz for hours and hours.

Gabapentin tolerance as well as oxycodone tolerance plays a huge part with this method. You can probably only do this once or twice before your body adapts to the gabapentin dosage.  And of course having a high opioid tolerance to start with may affect the outcome as well. Took me a while to get it right. Months.

Experimentation  and dosage adjustment until you get it right.

Gabapentin tolerance happens extremely quickly. So as I said, this only works once or twice until you have to stop the gabapentin for a few days if you can and then try it again. 

The dosages I used may be to high or to low depending on your own tolerances. Stay safe with doing this above all else. But once you get it right, its fantastic.

<!-- POST END: id=13996762 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14060420 num=797 author=Lifer711 author_id=452585 date=2017-06-14T04:06:14+0100 -->
### Post #797

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14060420 |
| Author | Lifer711 |
| Author ID | 452585 |
| Date | Jun 14, 2017 at 4:06 AM |
| Page | 40 |

Definitely stagger these boys. Every 30 mins or so with an aleve or two and a carbonated drink, coke, whatever. Plus high fat meals also add to the effect.


Naproxen Sodium increases absorption 12-15% and believe me it's noticeable. But most importantly staggering every 30-45 mins will give you a much greater effect instead of swallowing 2400 mg at one time.


As far as effects go, I would describe it like being drunk motor skill wise, but your brain is still fairly clear. On higher doses, I notice some things are more vibrant and music tends to sound a lot better. Booze will make the high really sloppy though, try to limit it to just a beer or 2.


On the potentiating/synergistic side, tramadol has a fantastic synergistic effect, although if taking large doses is recommend a benzo of some sort, either a 1 mg alprazolam or preferably a 1 or 2 mg clonazepam goes really well. Just wanna keep an eye on that seizure threshold.


Only cons I've really noticed is like what has been posted in earlier threads, tolerance builds extremely quickly. It's best to maybe dose for a day or two in a row, then wait a week. Keep that tolerance at bay and let your mind reset.


I've never noticed much withdrawal, especially on a methadone/heroin withdrawal level, not even in the same fucking realm lol. Maybe a slight bummed out feeling, but you won't be in the fetal position, dry heaving and shitting your insides out like a cold turkey 180 mg methadone withdrawal....*shudders* lol.

<!-- POST END: id=14060420 -->

### Post #800

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14060871 |
| Author | Jabberwocky |
| Author ID | 520884 |
| Date | Jun 14, 2017 at 5:49 PM |
| Page | 40 |

Is the question that you took 4500mg of gabapentin and 30 minutes later you're not feeling anything? 


If you haven't taken gabapentin before, that is a good enough of a dose to get a feeling of how the drug affects you. Some people don't find anything particularly enjoyable or significant about gabapentin. If one has a tolerance to stuff like benzos or alcohol then there might be something like cross tolerance. 


Wait some more to see what happens. It can take a little while to really kick in sometimes, or at least for the effects to be noticeable (going for a walk can make the effects more obvious). Keep in mind gabapentin is really nothing like tramadol, so don't expect the same kinds of effects.

<!-- POST END: id=14060871 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14061053 num=808 author=Jekyl Anhydride author_id=416049 date=2017-06-14T21:33:48+0100 -->
### Post #808

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Author | Jekyl Anhydride |
| Author ID | 416049 |

> [Shawsheen said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=14060869)
> 
> 
> 
> 			The reason is Gabapentin. I'm totally knew to it and literally just got it and took a bunch. WAY more than recommended by almost everybody. I took 4500mg an hour and 30 minutes ago and I feel nothing so far.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Shawsheen said:


Hey Shawnsheen, Welcome to BL. Gabapentin can be a very subtle drug, where it really shines is aiding in withdrawal from opioids and to a degree benzos IMO. The transporter system in your GI tract/ gut responsible for absorbing gabapentin is easily saturated by high levels and will only let so much into your bloodstream at one time. Anything over about a gram /1000mg during any 30 min period will just dose your toilet. While eating a little protein & fat and/or taking Naproxen sodium (Alleve) can help, the best method is to just take some in a stagger, every 20-40 mins. Also taking four+ grams at once can cause unpleasant diarrhea IME. Personally I prefer 800mg every 30mins, it takes about 90 mins to start reaching full effect and lasts for a few hours depending on stagger time. Your mileage may vary.


On a side note be careful when taking "tons" of Tramadol. It carries the risk of seizures in doses above 400mg. No bueno.

<!-- POST END: id=14061053 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14061382 num=812 author=Jekyl Anhydride author_id=416049 date=2017-06-15T06:22:33+0100 -->
### Post #812

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14061382 |
| Author | Jekyl Anhydride |
| Author ID | 416049 |
| Date | Jun 15, 2017 at 6:22 AM |
| Page | 41 |

No that's a good stagger, you might want to eat a snack or have a small glass of milk. As strange as that sounds Gabapentin is treated like an amino acid in your system and fat/ protein actually helps with absorption as well as naproxen sodium. After that if you still don't get much out of it you might have to accept that it's not going to do much for you. It's a strange drug and in some it can be very mild compared to benzos or opioids. If your daily regimen already contains other gabaergic meds then I would feel even more certain about the previous statement. Give it some time but don't be disappointed if it doesn't rock your world.

<!-- POST END: id=14061382 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14061428 num=813 author=Shawsheen author_id=452631 date=2017-06-15T07:04:52+0100 -->
### Post #813

| Field | Value |

Oppie1025, I leaned literally today that the most unique thing about Gabapentin is that you can literally take too much, and it actually makes it not work at all. I'm new to Gabapentin, and if you read my posts from earlier today I recorded what I took, when, and the result. I took 4,500mg and it didn't work.......several hours later I took 2,400mg and Xanax cause I hear that might help achieving the desired high. It was a huge mistake. I took all of those and just fell asleep for 4 hours.....,no high, no fun. However, around 11pm, my ridiculous, dangerous, and stupid Irish stubbornness kicked in and I was like, "F" it! Screw it! Do I took more, but this time Intook 2,400mg on its own with no Xanax. The calm, relaxed euphoria I spent all day trying to find has FINALLY arrived mildly.........just 12 freaking hours too late. Anyway, there are a lot of people writing and responding about Gabapentin that know WAY more than me. BUT, the one thing I can swear by is that if you take too much it becomes legitimately null and void........for whatever reason it did not work at all. Most drugs the more you take the more fun you have.......Gabapentin is fussy, difficult, and strange. Nevertheless, I will make another attempt with it at some point. There are, in deed, great stories many about people having great times taking it. Thus, my advice, although I'm probably not that authorized to really give advice since today was the first time I took Gabapentin too. Despite that, I am convinced and can almost promise you, that Gabapentin require kinda strick ways to take it. Plenty of knowledgeable people claim they know the secret" (ha). Some are probably right. Anyway, the only DEFINITE thing I can add is that more does not mean better. There are certain amounts of Gabapentin that work and other's don't. I suggest a little adventure to find the most honest, experienced, and knowledgeable  person you can find. There is the correct way to take it and you get a nice euphoric high; I've been around people on it......trust me, they're having fun. Lastly, a reminder, and this is the one thing that a Gabapentin rookie knows for a fact.,,,,,,,,taking a TON of it, specifically, I took throughout  the day, a total of 11,400mg.......and only right now I feel slightly sedated, calm, and comfortable.......but still not high. I hope my mistakes help you out. Best of luck, amigo

| Date | Jun 15, 2017 at 3:48 PM |
| Page | 41 |

I woke up, took 2400mg and pretty much got what I was looking for with the Gabapentin (sort of). No euphoria, unfortunately, but I am in a great mood. I shaved, showered, put on some nice clothes, and had that "ready to face the day" feeling. Look, I'll take what I can get (ha). I'm a writer.......,,..specializing and focusing mainly on speech writing, on assisting high school kids with the writing portion of the SAT, and helping high school kids with their college essays, as well as helping college kids with their essays to get into graduate school and medical school. I only mention this just because it's important that I have a positive "let's start the day kind of attitude" when I meet with clients........particularly because my clients are scared, nervous, and feel like they're under a tremendous amount of pressure. Did you guys know that valid and legitimate studies tell us that the second most feared thing by Americans (after death, of course) is, in fact, public speaking? I mention this because it's very important that I exude a calm, relaxed confidence in these situations..,,,,,and I'll be honest, prescription drugs help. Tramadol is the BEST for that.....,I save it for the highest paying jobs......that will usually involve assisting someone running for office or a retirement speech from someone who ran a large and successful company that has anywhere from hundreds to thousands of employees. I also take a TON of Xanax and even opioids on rare occasions. To be perfectly honest, I'd like to take illegal drugs, but I'm too scared to get in trouble. Being arrested for buying drugs would make a TON of people not hire me.......so I get all my prescription drugs from generous doctors. Anyway, I got off track. Like I said, I'm in a great mood, but I am angry that I wasted all that Gabapentin yesterday. From reading what different people wrote, it seemed like toothpastedog and Jekyl Anhydride seemed to have interesting ideas. Jekyl Anhydride seemed to have a real systematic approach that he thought would breed success with Gabapentin. I'll pay attention to the things he said and hopefully says again.......maybe they'll work for me! Toothpastedog shares the same skepticism I have........the thought that, "hey, it just might not work for you"........he seems to know what he's talking about and is probably right, BUT, I'm not giving up yet!.......which is probably stupid. I'll look for suggestions from Jekyl Anhydride, and any others with suggestions on how to take Gabapentin and, well, essentially get high.......

<!-- POST START: id=14072782 num=817 author=Scrofula author_id=447162 date=2017-06-28T07:58:52+0100 -->
### Post #817

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14072782 |
| Author | Scrofula |
| Author ID | 447162 |
| Date | Jun 28, 2017 at 7:58 AM |
| Page | 41 |

Indeed they do, I do in fact.  Not as such, it was prescribed more as a "please leave my office" thing, but I continue to take it since it's done more for me than years of sertraline/Zoloft or booze have done.


Script is 600mg x  3/day.  Typically I actually take 2400mg/day, which means I run out before the month is up.  I pretend that I do this intentionally to prevent tolerance from developing.


It is quite good for my run-of-the-mill social phobias, and the more general angst about life.  I don't really get, and don't know, probably wouldn't help with, acute panic attacks or nasty cases of agoraphobia or anything.  In fact, it's so glacially slow it would probably be one of the last to be recommended for attacks.


If you want to be say, more talkative at the company picnic and seem sober, really just 1200mg works (no tolerance) for me, and probably less is still effective.  

That's definitely the threshold for that "sense of well-being" some people call a "high" and get the kids all excited about.


Of course, some people fall asleep at 300, and others don't react at all.  It is a strange one.

<!-- POST END: id=14072782 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14073534 num=824 author=Jabberwocky author_id=520884 date=2017-06-29T04:36:18+0100 -->

| Author ID | 520884 |

I haven't read of gabapentin use itself causing seizures. It's a pretty benign medication. The withdrawal from it if you become dependent might lower the seizure threshold, but using it doesn't seem to. Unlike pregabalin, where higher doses can cause a seizure. The subjective experience of pregabalin and gabapentin have a lot in common though.

<!-- POST END: id=14073534 -->

I admit I haven't and probably won't do that search.  Just look at the URLS to these stories, or at the ads on the page, and you'll get an idea.  I think class-action lawyers copypasta random drugs and diseases to find clients. 


Gabapentin and pregabalin are both anti-epilepsy, reviewed: [https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5114206/](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5114206/)


A survey of epilepsy specialists in 2017: "Compared to the 2005 and 2001 surveys, there was increased preference for the use of levetiracetam and lamotrigine, and decreased preference for the use of phenytoin, gabapentin, phenobarbital and carbamazepine."


But then, *high doses* of lots of things might cause a seizure.


Haven't tried pregabalin/Lyrica, but my understanding is they fixed a lot of the kinetics problems.  Meaning it's more potent.  Otherwise same mechanism.


Your gabapentin experience would just be a bit milder than the pregabalin, and take three hours longer to happen.  BUT it's whole lot cheaper, at least. 


I don't know why food would come up.  I don't get munchies or anything.  You do not have to eat weird things with them, or anything at all.

<!-- POST START: id=14073908 num=828 author=Jabberwocky author_id=520884 date=2017-06-29T17:53:49+0100 -->
### Post #828

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14073908 |
| Author | Jabberwocky |
| Author ID | 520884 |
| Date | Jun 29, 2017 at 5:53 PM |
| Page | 42 |

It is hardly guaranteed, but a high enough dose probably could lower your seizure threshold. But that would be a massive dose, exponentially higher than what one would normally be tolerant to. Pregabalin gets into issues over 600mg, but gapabentin doesn't seem to get into particularly dangerous territory even at 10,000mg. 


If one was already prone to seizures or has had them before, I'd suggest being caution just because it is the smart thing to do. But from what know about gabapentin it isn't a significant issue like it is with something like tramadol or pregabalin.

<!-- POST END: id=14073908 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=14073924 num=829 author=Scrofula author_id=447162 date=2017-06-29T18:15:08+0100 -->
### Post #829

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14073924 |
| Author | Scrofula |
| Author ID | 447162 |
| Date | Jun 29, 2017 at 6:15 PM |
| Page | 42 |

Yeah, Mr. Dob, these things don't cause seizures at any level, unless you mixed with other drugs or had a seizure disorder already.  This includes gabapentin and pregabalin/Lyrica.  


The exception is tiagebine, which is what you were taking when you had your seizures.  Overdoses of that are associated with seizures.  It works in a completely different way from gabapentin and pregabalin and benzos.


So: 

Tiagebine OD: seizures maybe

Gabapentin OD: no seizures

Pregabalin OD: no seizures

Benzo OD: no seizures

Lamictal OD: no seizures

<!-- POST END: id=14073924 -->

Gabapentin has generic manufacturers now and is relatively cheap and being unscheduled, receiving multiple scripts wouldn't be overly difficult. I went through a similar dose escalation like Toothpastedog and while I didn't quite reach 20g I was way up there for 8-9 months and payed for it with a rather prolonged nasty withdrawal syndrome that cost me a pretty cool friend on this site. Although I wasn't using it at first and did have a years worth saved up or my habit would have been more conservative.


 Point being it really does build tolerance insanely fast and I get more out of it by using it in week long spurts but I'm not using it for herpes zoster neuropathy or anything like that.

<!-- POST START: id=14104588 num=840 author=Jabberwocky author_id=520884 date=2017-08-06T18:15:43+0100 -->
### Post #840

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14104588 |
| Author | Jabberwocky |
| Author ID | 520884 |
| Date | Aug 6, 2017 at 6:15 PM |
| Page | 42 |

The high from that dose is essentially the same as a "more reasonable" dose of like 4g, only point of taking so much is tolerance. And even then the effects aren't particularly strong. I tend to prefer the effects of gabapentin to pregabalin though. Side effects of high doses of pregabalin were rather odd and uncomfortable (and high doses of pregabalin are more like at and over 900mg, not multiple grams), whereas I didn't notice any similar degree of uncomfortable side effects with those unreasonably high doses of gabapentin.

### Post #848

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14113790 |
| Author | Cody57Drine? |
| Author ID | 459737 |
| Date | Aug 18, 2017 at 8:04 AM |
| Page | 43 |

Gabapentin is an anti-convulsant prescribed for those with seizures and restless leg syndrome, among other first-line uses. I am prescribed for the off-label use to treat anxiety, but it's completely different than benzos. In terms of heightening its effect I'm not positive, but my initial thinking is that any way to augment it is very mild, or perhaps, psychological. I have tried snorting it, and have loaded up on it, but it honestly wasn't much different in feeling than taking 300-600. I wanted to get off klonopin and replace it with a non-controlled substance, and it's really worked for me. So if you're looking to get "high" off it, I don't find it really works that way. But, if you need to calm down, or mellow out, it really is a great, safe, way to get that.

<!-- POST END: id=14113790 -->

### Post #855

| Page | 43 |

So I've been experimenting with gabapentin over the last three months. Between 2014 and may of 2017 i used various benzos medicinally and recreationally. 

Tolerance to gaba like drugs is a bitch. This effected gabapentin efficacy tremendously. 


Today I took 1800mg total staggered over about an hour and a half about 45min after dinner. about two and a half hours after dosing I felt very warm in my face and a slight headache but nothing that resembled euphoria, I actually started to get intense cravings to drink alcohol, but luckily I didn't give in to them. 


About three and a half hours after dosing I smoked a tiny bit of pot and ate some protein and bam... I started to feel the more positive effects, mood elevation, sociability etc, but nothing that was major... just a subtle feeling good. 


As I write this it's been roughly 6 hours since I dosed and I feel slightly energetic but not anxious.

Conclusions: gabapentin is a strange drug. The come up takes forever, and one has to really plan their day around taking it to achieve the desired effects at the right time.  I'm interested in exploring higher doses but I feel the effects are too subtle to have any meaningful recreational value if taken alone. I really suggest smoking pot with it

<!-- POST END: id=14142910 -->

Gabapentin acts on anxiety & depression by blocking  calcium channel-mediated release of stress hormone catecholamines (epinephrine & norepinephrine) by the adrenal glands when triggered by nerve impulses from the amygdala in your brain after a threat is perceived. A threat can be a predator near you, something remembered or something heard.

**Hello, I was wondering if someone could help?**


> [D's said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=7460980)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Hey!!!! Let me tell you some stuff about Gabapentin(Neurontin).
> 
> **What is it?-**Gabapentin (Neurontin) is a GABA analogue. It was originally developed for the treatment of epilepsy, and currently, Gabapentin is widely used to relieve pain, especially neuropathic pain.
> 
> 
> 
> ![220px-Gabapentin_3D.png](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F7%2F7b%2FGabapentin_3D.png%2F220px-Gabapentin_3D.png&hash=7d86e4c09b9b081d2a2236657dc7d2de)
> 
> **So why was it made?**Gabapentin was initially synthesized to mimic the chemical structure of the neurotransmitter gamma-aminobutyric acid (GABA), but is not believed to act on the same brain receptors.**Sounds a lot like GHB/GBL****GHB-gamma-Hydroxybutyric acid, a neuroprotective and depressant drug**&**GBL-gamma-Butyrolactone** Hmmmm.. They sound very alike!
> 
> **What's it feel like?-**It varies from person to person. I don't want to tell you to go out and take 2500+mg.. Begin with a low dose to see how it effects you. I'm no MD but I can tell you that if it's your first time you should begin with 1-3 to begin with (900mg). It has the same sort of effect's of xanax, ghb, and hydrocodone. With a THC buzz. It makes me feel really dream like, and smooth high. When I take high doses I tend to drop things, and have a small twitching problem. 
> 
> **Best way to take it!-**I don't want you to go and do this to every gabapen capsule you have. I normally will empty the contents of the capsules into a square of toilet paper and parachute it. It tastes **WORST** than ecstasy/mdma! Gabapentin tastes horable!!! So be sure to swallow it before it bust's open in your mouth!
> 
> **Cool things about Gabapentin!-**There have been reports by methamphetamine addicts that gabapentin alone in doses of 1200 mg at bedtime taken for 40–60 days has been effective in reducing the withdrawal symptoms and almost eliminating cravings or desire to use methamphetamine. It also helps those addicted to prescribed pain medications and takes away withdrawal symptoms.
> 
> **Is it addictive?**-Yes, it is. it's withdrawl effects are verry similar to benzo/alocohol withdrawl symptoms. (Only after long term use.)
> 
> **So what's it feel like again...?-**Although gabapentin is not a controlled substance, it does produce psychoactive effects that could lead to recreational use of the drug. However, it is widely regarded as having little or no potential for misuse. Pregabalin, a gabapentinoid with higher potency marketed for neuropathic pain, is a controlled substance, under Schedule V of the United States' Controlled Substances Act.
> 
> Recreational use of gabapentin produces a varying number of effects including euphoria, appetite stimulation, incessant talking, physical and mental stimulation which result in varying degrees of drug-induced productivity. Diarrhea/stomach discomfort is commonly reported with heavy use.
> 
> *Gabapentin is close to pregabalin(lyrica)*
> 
> If you have any questions, comments, complaints, or what you experience with gabapentin, please let us know!!!!
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — D's said:

<!-- POST START: id=14281063 num=870 author=Scrofula author_id=447162 date=2018-03-04T05:43:30+0000 -->
### Post #870

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14281063 |
| Author | Scrofula |
| Author ID | 447162 |
| Date | Mar 4, 2018 at 5:43 AM |
| Page | 44 |

Just FYI, the point of returns-that're-more-trouble-than-they're-worth is probably above 2400mg/day.  If you're new to it and don't feel anything pleasant at that dose, you never will; if you feel good at that dose, you won't feel any better with more.  You'll just start dosing the toilet and reduce your tolerance further.


So of course I've done at least 3600mg over 16 hours or so, not at the beginning of fresh non-tolerance.  Really no added benefit, def. doesn't make me barf.


But then at the usual 1800mg, I can get higher than any prescription, abused or otherwise, that I've otherwise abused or tried, seemingly at random.  Still didn't make me barf though.  


And another but, there are people who say 100mg puts them to sleep, so it's definitely got a range of reactions*.


As for barfing and then immediately feeling better, you have gotten drunk and barfed before, right?  Or ate something nasty, fought it, gave in and barfed, and immediately felt better?  Yeah, that's how people's bodies work, nothing unusual about that.  


Your brain will actively work to make you feel terrible in order to get you to barf, since it detects some chemical in your blood it thinks is poison, and is usually right.  So besides the relief of your brain shutting up, it'll sometimes reward you with a shot of endorphins, you know, for your trouble.


---


[table="width: 500, align: right"]

[tr="bgcolor: white"]

[td]*Still think it's more like a bimodal or trimodal set of reactions: 2 or 3 different populations, maybe some SNP somewhere, so that you have strong-reactors, non-reactors, and high-as-fuck reactors.  


But then, people say they get high on benzos, and I just don't believe them.[/td]

[/tr]

[/table]

<!-- POST START: id=14285984 num=874 author=Jekyl Anhydride author_id=416049 date=2018-03-10T01:53:54+0000 -->
### Post #874

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Author | Jekyl Anhydride |
| Author ID | 416049 |
